Mon 11/02/2015 at 10:24 AM

From yesterday Hewlett-Packard made a spin off into 2 companies - Hewlett Packard Enterprise Comp (HPE) and HP Inc. (HPQ). In the fund LCF - Spekoliunas' Diversified Hedge Fund (https://portfolio.marketocracy.com/?page=03-01-00-001&fund=4167-10) I own Hewlett-Packard since August and I can see that spin off still isn't realized in Marketocracy and in my fund of course.

http://www.hpalumni.org/split
Stock and options

Stock. Each stockholder will receive one share of Hewlett Packard Enterprise stock (new stock symbol HPE) for each share of HP (unchanged stock symbol HPQ.) -- therefore, your basis cost will be split 50/50. Stockholders will receive cash in lieu of fractional shares. Stockholders do not need to take any action.  Press Release Oct 1 

http://www8.hp.com/us/en/hp-news/press-release.html?wireId=1989059&pageTitle=HP+Board+of+Directors+Approves+Separation+#.VjecUuk4o3Z
one share of HPE for each share of HPQ held 

HPQ symbol remains but the name will be changed to Hwelett Packard Inc. 
October 21, 2015, the record date   20151021
HPE is the spin off stock   Hewlett Packard Enterprise.
